	var loginStatusResponse;
	var loginResponseSet = false;
	var loginHandlers = new Array();

    function loadLogin(json) {
		loginStatusResponse = json;
        if (json.loginStatus.loggedIn) {
            if (json.loginStatus.accessProfile) {
                $('#profileLogoutPanel').removeClass("hidden");
                $('#logoutPanel').addClass("hidden");
                $('#loginRegisterPanel').addClass("hidden");
				$('.register').addClass("hidden");
                $('#username1').text( json.loginStatus.screenname );
            } else {
                $('#profileLogoutPanel').addClass("hidden");
                $('#logoutPanel').removeClass("hidden");
                $('#loginRegisterPanel').addClass("hidden");
				$('.register').removeClass("hidden");
                $('#username2').text( json.loginStatus.screenname );
            }
                        $('#subscribeNLWidgetLoggedOut').addClass("hidden");
            $('#subscribeNLWidgetLoggedIn').removeClass("hidden");
			
						if(json.loginStatus.askedCookiePolicy && json.loginStatus.acceptsCookiePolicy){
				$('#euCookiesQuestion').hide();
				$("body > header").css('margin', '0px auto 0px');
			}
												if(jQuery.cookie('acceptsCookies')=='accepts') {		
				$('#euCookiesQuestion').hide();
				$("body > header").css('margin', '0px auto 0px');
			}
			
        } else {
            $('#loginRegisterPanel').removeClass("hidden");
			$('.register').removeClass("hidden");
            $('#logoutPanel').addClass("hidden");
            $('#profileLogoutPanel').addClass("hidden");
            $('#subscribeNLWidgetLoggedIn').addClass("hidden");
            $('#subscribeNLWidgetLoggedOut').removeClass("hidden");
			
						if(jQuery.cookie('at')!=null) {		
				jQuery.cookie("at", null, { 
				path: '/', 
				expires: -5, 
				domain: '.' + location.host.replace('www.','').replace('m.','') });
				console.info('pluck cookie removed');
				console.info(jQuery.cookie('at'));
							}
									if(jQuery.cookie('acceptsCookies')=='accepts') {		
				$('#euCookiesQuestion').hide();
				$("body > header").css('margin', '0px auto 0px');
			}
			
        }

		loginResponseSet = true;
		$(document).trigger('loginResponse');		
    }
    
    				$(document).ready(function() {
    	if (($.cookie("sessionKey") == null) && ($.cookie("rememberMe") == null) ) {
    		loadLogin({loginStatus:{loggedIn:false}});
    	} else {
            $.getJSON('/ajax?action=loginStatus', loadLogin);
    	}
	});

              <div class="article-content m20-b KonaBody">
                <p>
                  <b>
                    <!--PSTYLE=$ID/[No paragraph style]-->                  </b>
                </p>
                <p>
                  THE success of the Glasgow Commonwealth Games could be the catalyst for a Scottish bid to host the Euro 2024 football championships, Tory leader Ruth Davidson has said.
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
                <p>
                  The city has proved it is capable of holding a major international sporting events, according to the Glasgow MSP.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Ms Davidson added: “Glasgow 2014 has been sensational - let’s build on our success to land other major sports tournaments and show the world what Scotland can do.”
                </p>
                <p>
                  <strong>
                    • 
                    <a href="http://www.scotsman.com/sport/live-blog-commonwealth-games-2014-1-3487434" title="Link to blog">
                      Follow the Commonwealth Games day-by-day with our live blog
                    </a>
                  </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                  The Tories have set out a number of suggestions which could make the bid for the 24-team tournament feasible. This includes focussing the contest on Celtic Park, Hampden, Ibrox and Murrayfield, while upgrading smaller stadia in Edinburgh, Aberdeen and Dundee and Kilmarnock. Some matches could also be staged in the north of England.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Glasgow is already bidding to be one of the host cities in the 2020 European championships which will be staged in a unique 60th anniversary touring format in cities across 13 different countries.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Ms Davidson added: “If the format reverts to the usual process in 2024, we know from the last 10 days or so that Scotland is more than capable of being a superb host.
                </p>
                <p>
                  “Scotland’s are the best fans in the world, a fact acknowledged globally, and are deserving of an event like this on their doorstep.
                </p>
                <p>
                  “We’ve already got four world-class grounds in Glasgow and Edinburgh, with the opportunity of expanding several more across the country  – not uncommon for a major football tournament.”
                </p>
                <p>
                  Matches could be staged across the border in the North of England with Newcastle and Sunderland staging matches, he added.
                </p>
                <p>
                  Scotland lost out in a joint-bid with Ireland to stage the 2008 European Championships.
                </p>
                <p>
                  <strong>
                    SEE ALSO
                  </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                  <strong>
                    • 
                    <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=C1birs_ec4Y" title="Commonwealth Games">
                      Scotsman Commonwealth Games live discussions
                    </a>
                  </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                  <strong>
                    • 
                    <a href="http://www.scotsman.com/sport/team-scotland-s-commonwealth-games-medal-total-1-3488805" title="Link to table">
                      Medal table: What medals have Team Scotland won?
                    </a>
                  </strong>
                </p>
                <p>
                </p>
              </div>

                            <div class="pluck-comm-comment-content">
                              <div class="pluck-comm-rate-system">
                                <span class="pluck-score-volume pluck-score-has-info" upvotes="11" downvotes="2" volume="9" activity="13" scoreontargetkey="CommentKey:67fda1ce-5779-49c1-a5ef-57cda76cf03f">

                              <h4 class="pluck-comm-username-url pluck-comm-username-withheld">
                                <span>
                                  Name withheld
                                </span>
                              </h4>
                              <h4 class="pluck-comm-username-url pluck-comm-username-display">
                                <!-- <a href="http://www.scotsman.com/community/persona.html?UID=4196010695c0c040f8a1b5a943277d2bcffcab507162010a8e8a3c255798ea57&plckUserId=4196010695c0c040f8a1b5a943277d2bcffcab507162010a8e8a3c255798ea57"> -->                                Damian Thirsty
                                <!-- </a> -->                              </h4>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-timestamp">
                                12:59 PM on 01/08/2014
                              </p>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-ignoredmsg">
                                <em>
                                  This comment is hidden because you have chosen to ignore Damian Thirsty.
                                </em>
                                <a class="pluck-comm-show-hidden-info" href="#">
                                  Show Details
                                </a>
                                <a class="pluck-comm-hide-hidden-info" href="#">
                                  Hide Details
                                </a>
                              </p>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-abusereportedmsg">
                                <em>
                                  This comment is hidden because you have submitted an abuse report against it.
                                </em>
                                <a class="pluck-comm-show-hidden-info" href="#">
                                  Show Details
                                </a>
                                <a class="pluck-comm-hide-hidden-info" href="#">
                                  Hide Details
                                </a>
                              </p>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-body">
                                Sadly Scotland doesn't have the required stadia to succesfully host such a tourney Ibrox and Parkhead are suitable but no other tournaments have used multiple stadiums in the same city as there ends up being too many fans so the matches have to be distributed.
                                <br/>
                                <br/>
                                 A new Hampden should be built in Stirling (with a national football centre similar to the one England has) as it has clearly long past its sell-by bate as the 3rd best stadium in Glasgow.
                                <br/>
                                <br/>
                                 Murrayfield could be used in Edinburgh and Pittodrie would be OK for smaller matches in Aberdeen.
                                <br/>
                                <br/>
                                 Dundee and Dundee Utd should sell both grounds and build a new one which was capable of holding the required numbers though.
                                <br/>
                                <br/>
                                 Then we would be in a better position to host this.
                              </p>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-score-action-error pluck-error-message">

                              </p>
                              <p class="pluck-comm-score-general-error pluck-error-message">
                                We are unable to record your recommendation at this time. Please try again later.
                              </p>

              <script type="text/javascript">
//<![CDATA[

				$('#findTabs-2 #findItSearchButton').bind('click',function(event){
					event.preventDefault();
			        event.stopPropagation();
					performFindItSearch();
				});	
				
				$('#findTabs-2 input[type=text]').enterPressed(function(event) {
					event.preventDefault();
			        event.stopPropagation();
					performFindItSearch();
				});
			
				function performFindItSearch(){
					var where = $('#findTabs-2 #directoryWhere').val();
					var what = $('#findTabs-2 #directoryKeywords').val();
					where = where.replace(/\s+/g, '-').toLowerCase();
					what = what.replace(/\s+/g, '-').toLowerCase();
					var searchBaseURL = 'http://www.scotsman.com' + '/findit/search';
					var altURL;
										if(altURL && altURL.length > 0){
						searchBaseURL = altURL;
					}
					window.open(searchBaseURL + '/' + escape(where) + '/'+escape(what), '_blank');
				};	
			
//]]>
              </script>

        <div class="moreContainer">
          <div class="moreInfo">
            <ul class="headers">
              <li data="C1">
                <h3>
                  What is a Cookie?
                </h3>
              </li>
              <li data="C2">
                <h3>
                  What is a Flash Cookie?
                </h3>
              </li>
              <li data="C3">
                <h3>
                  Can I opt out of receiving Cookies?
                </h3>
              </li>
              <li data="C4">
                <h3>
                  About our Cookies
                </h3>
              </li>
            </ul>
            <ul class="cookieContent">
              <li rel="C1" class="content">
                <p>
                  Cookies are small data files which are sent to your browser (Internet Explorer, Firefox, Chrome etc) from a website you visit. They are stored on your electronic device.
                </p>
              </li>
              <li rel="C2" class="content">
                <p>
                  This is a type of cookie which is collected by Adobe Flash media player (it is also called a Local Shared Object) - a piece of software you may already have on your electronic device to help you watch online videos and listen to podcasts.
                </p>
              </li>
              <li rel="C3" class="content">
                <p>
                  Yes there are a number of options available, you can set your browser either to reject all cookies, to allow only "trusted" sites to set them, or to only accept them from the site you are currently on.
                </p>
                <p>
                  However, please note - if you block/delete all cookies, some features of our websites, such as remembering your login details, or the site branding for your local newspaper may not function as a result.
                </p>
              </li>
              <li rel="C4" class="content">
                <p>
                  The types of cookies we, our ad network and technology partners use are listed below:
                </p>
                <ul class="cookieList">
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Revenue Science 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      A tool used by some of our advertisers to target adverts to you based on pages you have visited in the past. To opt out of this type of targeting you can visit the 'Your Online Choices' website by 
                      <a href="http://www.youronlinechoices.com/uk/opt-out-help" target="_blank">
                        clicking here.
                      </a>
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Google Ads 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      Our sites contain advertising from Google; these use cookies to ensure you get adverts relevant to you. You can tailor the type of ads you receive by 
                      <a href="http://www.google.com/ads/preferences/" target="_blank">
                        visiting here
                      </a>
                       or to opt out of this type of targeting you can visit the 'Your Online Choices' website by 
                      <a href="http://www.youronlinechoices.com/uk/opt-out-help" target="_blank">
                        clicking here.
                      </a>
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Webtrends / Google Analytics 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      This is used to help us identify unique visitors to our websites. This data is anonymous and we cannot use this to uniquely identify individuals and their usage of the sites.
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Dart for Publishers 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      This comes from our ad serving technology and is used to track how many times you have seen a particular ad on our sites, so that you don't just see one advert but an even spread. This information is not used by us for any other type of audience recording or monitoring.
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      ComScore 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      ComScore monitor and externally verify our site traffic data for use within the advertising industry. Any data collected is anonymous statistical data and cannot be traced back to an individual.
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Local Targeting 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      Our Classified websites (Photos, Motors, Jobs and Property Today) use cookies to ensure you get the correct local newspaper branding and content when you visit them. These cookies store no personally identifiable information.
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Grapeshot 
                      <span>
                        ►
                      </span>
                    </h4>
                    <p>
                      We use Grapeshot as a contextual targeting technology, allowing us to create custom groups of stories outside out of our usual site navigation. Grapeshot stores the categories of story you have been exposed to. Their privacy policy and opt out option can be 
                      <a href="http://www.grapeshot.co.uk/privacy.html" target="_blank">
                        accessed here.
                      </a>
                    </p>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                    <h4>
                      Subscriptions Online 
                      <span>
                        ►

					$(document).ready(function(){
					setTimeout(function(){
					if ($("#wowf").length > 0) {
					if (document.cookie.indexOf("wowfCookieA") >= 0){
					$("#wowf").hide();
					}else{
					$('#wowf').lightbox_me({
                    zIndex: 10002,
					overlayCSS: ({background: "#000", opacity: "0.85", position: "fixed"}),
					closeSelector: (".wowfClose"),
                    closeClick: false
					});
					$(".wowfClose, .btnBar a").click(function(){
					var date = new Date();
					var minutes = 7200; //60 * 24 = 1440 * 5 days = 7200
					date.setTime(date.getTime() + (minutes * 60 * 1000));
					jQuery.cookie("wowfCookieA", 1, {expires : date});
					});
					}
					}
					},100);
